Question: A computer routine was developed to generate two numbers (x,y) the first being a random number between 0 and 100 inclusive, and the second being less than or equal to the square root of the first. Each of the following pair satisfies the routine except
Choices:
  A: (99,10)
  B: (85,9)
  C: (50,7)
  D: (1,1)
  E: (1,0)
Response 0:
Thought:
  The second number (y) must be less than or equal to the square root of the first number (x).
  For (99,10), 10 is less than or equal to the square root of 99.
  For (85,9), 9 is less than or equal to the square root of 85.
  For (50,7), 7 is less than or equal to the square root of 50.
  For (1,1), 1 is less than or equal to the square root of 1.
  For (1,0), 0 is not less than or equal to the square root of 1.
  Therefore, the answer is E: (1,0).

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 2 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: If 75 percent of the employees of a certain company take a winter vacation, 40 percent take a winter and a summer vacation, and 20 percent take neither a winter nor a summer vacation, what Q percent of the employees take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation?
Choices:
  A: 5%
  B: 15%
  C: 25%
  D: 35%
  E: 45%
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that there are 100 employees in the company.
  75% of the employees take a winter vacation, which means 75 employees take a winter vacation.
  40% of the employees take a winter and a summer vacation, which means 40 employees take both vacations.
  20% of the employees take neither a winter nor a summer vacation, which means 20 employees take neither vacation.
  We can use this information to find the number of employees who take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation.
  Let's call this number Q.
  Q = (number of employees who take a summer vacation) - (number of employees who take both vacations)
  Q = (100% - 20%) - 40%
  Q = 80% - 40%
  Q = 40%
  Therefore, 40% of the employees take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation.
  The answer is D: 35%.
Action: Answer("D")

Topic: Math
Question: A rectangular solid, 3 x 4 x 15, is inscribed in a sphere, so that all eight of its vertices are on the sphere. What is the diameter of the sphere?
Choices:
  A:  13.3542
  B:  15.8113
  C:  18.3451
  D:  19.5667
  E:  20.8888
Response 0:
Thought:
  The rectangular solid has dimensions 3 x 4 x 15.
  The sphere is inscribed in the rectangular solid, so the diameter of the sphere is equal to the space diagonal of the rectangular solid.
  The space diagonal of the rectangular solid can be found using the Pythagorean theorem.
  The Pythagorean theorem states that the square of the space diagonal is equal to the sum of the squares of the three dimensions of the rectangular solid.
  Therefore, the diameter of the sphere is the square root of the sum of the squares of the three dimensions of the rectangular solid.
  The diameter of the sphere is the square root of (3^2 + 4^2 + 15^2) = 16.1555.
  The answer is not one of the choices given.
Action: Answer("None of the Above")

Topic: Math
Question: Peter wants to find 10 additional people to form a scavenger hunt team with him. If he has 10 friends who would like to participate, how many choices does he have for forming his team?
Choices:
  A: 0
  B: 1
  C: 2
  D: 3
  E: 4
Response 0:
Thought:
  Peter wants to find 10 additional people to form a scavenger hunt team with him.
  He has 10 friends who would like to participate.
  The number of ways to choose 10 people from 10 friends is 10 choose 10, which is equal to 1.
  Therefore, Peter has only 1 choice for forming his team.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 5 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Assistants are needed to prepare for preparation. Each helper can make either 2 large cakes or 35 small cakes/hr. The kitchen is available for 3 hours and 20 large cakes & 700 small cakes are needed. How many helpers are required?
Choices:
  A: 8
  B: 10
  C: 12
  D: 15
  E: 19
Response 0:
Thought:
- Each helper can make either 2 large cakes or 35 small cakes/hr.
- The kitchen is available for 3 hours, so the total number of hours available is 3 * 1 = 3 hours.
- We need to make 20 large cakes and 700 small cakes.
- Let's first calculate how many large cakes can be made in 3 hours by one helper: 2 large cakes/hour * 3 hours = 6 large cakes.
- To make 20 large cakes, we need 20 large cakes / 6 large cakes per helper = 3.33 helpers. We can't have a fraction of a helper, so we need 4 helpers to make 20 large cakes.
- Now let's calculate how many small cakes can be made in 3 hours by one helper: 35 small cakes/hour * 3 hours = 105 small cakes.
- To make 700 small cakes, we need 700 small cakes / 105 small cakes per helper = 6.67 helpers. We can't have a fraction of a helper, so we need 7 helpers to make 700 small cakes.
- The total number of helpers needed is 4 + 7 = 11.
- Therefore, the answer is B: 10.

Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Thought:
- Each helper can make either 2 large cakes or 35 small cakes/hr.
- The kitchen is available for 3 hours, so the total number of hours available is 3 * 1 = 3 hours.

- To make 700 small cakes, we need 700 small cakes / 105 small cakes per helper = 6.67 helpers. We can't have a fraction of a helper, so we need 7 helpers to make 700 small cakes.
- The total number of helpers needed is 4 + 7 = 11.
- Therefore, the answer is B: 10.

- Each helper can make either 2 large cakes or 35 small cakes/hr.
- The kitchen is available for 3 hours, so the total number of hours available is 3 * 1 = 3 hours.
- We need to make 20 large cakes and 700 small cakes.
- Let's first calculate how many large cakes can be made in 3 hours by one helper: 2 large cakes/hour * 3 hours = 6 large cakes.
- To make 20 large cakes, we need 20 large cakes / 6 large cakes per helper = 3.33 helpers. We can't have a fraction of a helper, so we need 4 helpers to make 20 large cakes.
- Now let's calculate how many small cakes can be made in 3 hours by one helper: 35 small cakes/hour * 3 hours = 105 small cakes.
- To make 700 small cakes, we need 700 small cakes / 105 small cakes per helper = 6.67 helpers. We can't have a fraction of a helper, so we need 7 helpers to make 700 small cakes.
- The total number of helpers needed is 4 + 7 = 11.
- Therefore, the answer is B: 10.

Action: Answer("B")

Topic: Math
Question: An express electric train takes exact three seconds to enter tunnel which is 1 mile long.
If train is traveling at 120 mile an hour, how long will it take to pass completely through the tunnel ?
Choices:
  A: 43 seconds
  B: 39 seconds
  C: 20 seconds
  D: 33 seconds
  E: 55 seconds
Response 0:
Thought:
  The train takes 3 seconds to enter the tunnel.
  The tunnel is 1 mile long.
  The train is traveling at 120 miles per hour.
  We need to find the time it takes for the train to pass completely through the tunnel.
  We can use the formula: time = distance / speed.
  The distance is 1 mile + 1 mile = 2 miles (since the train has to travel the length of the tunnel twice).
  We need to convert the speed to miles per second, so we divide by 3600 (the number of seconds in an hour).
  speed = 120 miles/hour / 3600 seconds/hour = 1/30 miles/second.
  time = distance / speed = 2 miles / (1/30 miles/second) = 60 seconds.
  Therefore, it will take 60 seconds for the train to pass completely through the tunnel.
Action: Answer("None of the Above")

Question: A bookshelf contains 45 books, 30 of which are hardcover and 20 of which are fiction. What is the maximum number of books that are both hardcover and fiction?
Choices:
  A: 10
  B: 15
  C: 18
  D: 20
  E: 30
Response 0:
Thought:
  We know that there are 45 books in total, 30 of which are hardcover and 20 of which are fiction.
  Let's assume that all 20 fiction books are hardcover. Then, the maximum number of books that are both hardcover and fiction would be 20.
  However, we know that there are only 30 hardcover books in total, so the maximum number of books that are both hardcover and fiction cannot be greater than 20.
  Therefore, the answer is A: 10.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 8 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An electric pole, 14 metres high, casts a shadow of 10 metres. Find the height of a tree that casts a shadow of 15 metres under similar conditions.
Choices:
  A: 21
  B: 22
  C: 20
  D: 23
  E: 24
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's use the concept of similar triangles to solve this problem.
  The ratio of the height of the pole to the length of its shadow is 14/10.
  Let x be the height of the tree.
  The ratio of the height of the tree to the length of its shadow is x/15.
  Since the triangles are similar, the ratios of corresponding sides are equal.
  Therefore, we can set up the proportion: 14/10 = x/15 and solve for x.
  Cross-multiplying, we get 10x = 14 * 15.
  Solving for x, we get x = 21.
  Therefore, the height of the tree is 21 meters.
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 9 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: At what price should the Karan mark a sewing machine that costs him Rs. 1200/- so that even after offering a 20% discount, he makes 20% profit?
Choices:
  A: 1,879
  B: 1,875
  C: 1,876
  D: 1,872
  E: 1,800
Response 0:
Thought:
  Karan wants to make a 20% profit even after offering a 20% discount.
  Let's assume the marked price is x.
  After a 20% discount, the selling price will be 0.8x.
  Karan wants to make a 20% profit on the cost price of Rs. 1200.
  Therefore, the selling price should be 1.2 times the cost price.
  That is, 1.2 * 1200 = 1440.
  We know that the selling price after a 20% discount is 0.8x.
  So, 0.8x = 1440.
  Therefore, x = 1800.
  Therefore, the marked price should be Rs. 1800.
Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Thought:
  Karan wants to make a 20% profit even after offering a 20% discount.
  Let's assume the marked price is x.
  After a 20% discount, the selling price will be 0.8x.
  Karan wants to make a 20% profit on the cost price of Rs. 1200.
  Therefore, the selling price should be 1.2 times the cost price.
  That is, 1.2 * 1200 = 1440.
  We know that the selling price after a 20% discount is 0.8x.
  So, 0.8x = 1440.
  Therefore, x = 1800.
  Therefore, the marked price should be Rs. 1800.

Topic: Math
Question: At a certain factory, 10 percent of the staplers produced on Monday were defective and 2 percent of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake. If 72 of the non-defective staplers were rejected, what was the number of staplers produced that day?
Choices:
  A: 4,000
  B: 4,200
  C: 4,500
  D: 4,800
  E: 5,000
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the factory produced x staplers on Monday.
  10% of the staplers produced on Monday were defective, so 0.1x staplers were defective.
  Therefore, 0.9x staplers were non-defective.
  2% of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake, so 0.02(0.9x) = 0.018x non-defective staplers were rejected.
  We know that 72 non-defective staplers were rejected, so 0.018x = 72.
  Solving for x, we get x = 4,000.
  Therefore, the number of staplers produced that day was 4,000.
  The answer is A: 4,000.
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 12 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: M men agree to purchase a gift for Rs. D. If 3 men drop out how much more will each have to contribute towards the purchase of the gift?
Choices:
  A: D/(M-3)
  B: MD/3
  C: M/(D-3)
  D: 3D/(M2-3M)
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Thought:
  Initially, M men agreed to purchase a gift for Rs. D.
  Therefore, each man would have to contribute D/M rupees.
  If 3 men drop out, then the total number of men who will contribute towards the purchase of the gift will be (M-3).
  Therefore, each man will have to contribute (D/(M-3)) rupees.
  The amount that each man will have to contribute more is (D/(M-3)) - (D/M) = D((1/M) - (1/(M-3))).
  Therefore, the answer is A: D/(M-3).
Action: Answer("A")

Question: Add: +45 and -30
Choices:
  A: -30
  B: +30
  C: 0
  D: 15
  E: -15
Response 0:
Thought:
  +45 means positive 45.
  -30 means negative 30.
  To add two numbers with different signs, we subtract the smaller absolute value from the larger absolute value and keep the sign of the larger number.
  The absolute value of 45 is larger than the absolute value of 30.
  Therefore, we subtract 30 from 45 and keep the sign of 45, which is positive.
  45 - 30 = 15.
  The answer is D: 15.
Action: Answer("D")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 15 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The events A and B are independent. The probability that event A occurs is 0.6, and the probability that at least one of the events A or B occurs is 0.96. What is the probability that event B occurs?
Choices:
  A: 0.5
  B: 0.6
  C: 0.7
  D: 0.8
  E: 0.9
Response 0:
Thought:
  P(A) = 0.6
  P(A or B) = 0.96
  Since A and B are independent, P(A and B) = P(A) * P(B)
  P(A or B) = P(A) + P(B) - P(A and B)
  Substituting the values, we get 0.96 = 0.6 + P(B) - (0.6 * P(B))
  Solving the equation, we get P(B) = 0.8
  Therefore, the probability that event B occurs is 0.8.
Action: Answer("D")

Question: The price of a product is reduced by 30% . By what percentage should it be increased to make it 100%
Choices:
  A: 41.86%
  B: 42.86%
  C: 43.86%
  D: 44.86%
  E: 45.86%
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the original price of the product is 100.
  After reducing the price by 30%, the new price becomes 70.
  Now, we need to find the percentage increase required to make it 100.
  Let's assume the percentage increase required is x.
  Then, the new price after the increase will be (70 * (1 + x/100)).
  We need to find the value of x that makes the new price equal to 100.
  Therefore, we can set up the following equation:
  70 * (1 + x/100) = 100
  Solving for x, we get x = 42.86
  Therefore, the percentage increase required to make the price 100 is 42.86%
  The answer is B: 42.86%

Topic: Math
Question: Two balls A and B rotate along a circular track. Ball A makes 2 full rotations in 26 minutes. Ball B makes 5 full rotation in 35 minutes. If they start rotating now from the same point, when will they be at the same starting point again?
Choices:
  A: 1 hour and 31 minutes
  B: 2 hour and 31 minutes
  C: 3 hour and 31 minutes
  D: 4 hour and 31 minutes
  E: 5 hour and 31 minutes
Response 0:
Thought:
  Ball A makes 2 full rotations in 26 minutes, so it makes 1 full rotation in 13 minutes.
  Ball B makes 5 full rotations in 35 minutes, so it makes 1 full rotation in 7 minutes.
  We need to find the least common multiple (LCM) of 13 and 7 to determine when they will be at the same starting point again.
  The LCM of 13 and 7 is 91.
  Therefore, they will be at the same starting point again after 91 minutes.
  The answer is A: 1 hour and 31 minutes.

Question: A flagstaff 17.5 metre high casts a shadow of length 40.25 metre. The height of building, which casts a shadow of length 28.75 metre under similar conditions will be :
Choices:
  A: 12 metre
  B: 12.5 metre
  C: 13.5 metre
  D: 14 metre
  E: 15 metre
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the height of the building is 'h' meters.
  According to the problem, the flagstaff is 17.5 meters high and casts a shadow of length 40.25 meters.
  We can set up a proportion to solve for 'h':
  height of flagstaff / length of shadow of flagstaff = height of building / length of shadow of building
  17.5 / 40.25 = h / 28.75
  Solving for 'h':
  h = (17.5 x 28.75) / 40.25
  h = 12.5
  Therefore, the height of the building is 12.5 meters.
  The answer is B: 12.5 meter.
Action: Answer("B")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 19 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Suppose you want to arrange your English, Hindi, Mathematics, History, Geography and Science books on a shelf. In how many ways can you do it ?
Choices:
  A: 520
  B: 720
  C: 920
  D: None
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Thought:
  The number of ways to arrange n distinct objects is n! (n factorial).
  There are 6 books to arrange.
  Therefore, the number of ways to arrange the books is 6! = 720.
  The answer is B: 720.
Action: Answer("B")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 20 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An exam is given in a certain class. The average (arithmetic mean) of the highest score and the lowest score is equal to x. If the average score for the entire class is equal to y and there are z students in the class, where z > 5, then in terms of x, y, and z, what is the average score for the class excluding the highest and lowest scorers?
Choices:
  A: (zy – 2x)/z
  B: (zy – 2)/z
  C: (zx – y)/(z – 2)
  D: (zy – 2x)/(z -2)
  E: (zy – x)/(z + 2)
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the highest score be H and the lowest score be L.
  The average of the highest and lowest scores is (H+L)/2.
  We know that (H+L)/2 = x.
  Therefore, H+L = 2x.
  Let the sum of all the scores be S.
  We know that the average score for the entire class is y.
  Therefore, S/z = y.
  We need to find the average score for the class excluding the highest and lowest scorers.
  Let the sum of all the scores excluding the highest and lowest scorers be E.
  We know that E = S - H - L.
  We need to find E/(z-2).
  We can substitute S = yz and H+L = 2x in the above equation to get:
  E/(z-2) = (yz - 2x)/(z-2).
  Therefore, the answer is D: (zy – 2x)/(z -2).
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:

Question: Silu and Meenu were walking on the road.
Silu said, "I weigh 51 Kgs. How much do you weigh?"
Meenu replied that she wouldn't reveal her weight directly as she is overweight.
But she said, "I weigh 29 Kgs plus half of my weight. "How much does Meenu weigh?
Choices:
  A: 12
  B: 28
  C: 27
  D: 58
  E: 91
Response 0:
Thought:
  Silu weighs 51 Kgs.
  Meenu weighs 29 Kgs plus half of her weight.
  Let's assume Meenu's weight is x.
  Then, Meenu's weight can be represented as x = 29 + x/2.
  Solving for x, we get x = 58.
  Therefore, Meenu weighs 58 Kgs.
  The answer is D: 58.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 22 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An astronaut weighing 211 pounds on Earth would weigh 182 pounds on Venus. The weight of the astronaut on Venus would be approximately what percent of the astronaut’s weight on Earth?
Choices:
  A: 50%
  B: 60%
  C: 70%
  D: 86%
  E: 90%
Response 0:
Thought:
  The astronaut weighs 211 pounds on Earth and 182 pounds on Venus.
  The weight on Venus is approximately 86% of the weight on Earth.
  To find out, we can divide the weight on Venus by the weight on Earth and multiply by 100 to get the percentage.
  (182/211) * 100 = 86%
  Therefore, the answer is D: 86%.
Action: Answer("D")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 23 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: At its maximum speed, a space shuttle can travel 700m high in 40 seconds. It will also take 5 seconds to pass a point. What then is the length of the space shuttle?
Choices:
  A: 50 m
  B: 75 m
  C: 100 m
  D: 125 m
  E: 150 m
Response 0:
Thought:
  The space shuttle travels 700m in 40 seconds.
  Therefore, its speed is 700/40 = 17.5 m/s.
  It takes 5 seconds to pass a point, so the length of the shuttle is the distance it travels in 5 seconds at its maximum speed.
  The distance it travels in 5 seconds is 17.5 m/s * 5 s = 87.5 m.
  Therefore, the length of the space shuttle is 87.5 m.
Action: Answer("None of the Above") 
The calculated length of the space shuttle is not one of the available choices.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 24 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Alice wants to put up fencing around three sides of her rectangular yard and leave one side of 10 meters unfenced. If the yard has an area of 240 square meters, how many meters of fencing does she need?
Choices:
  A: 58
  B: 62
  C: 66
  D: 70
  E: 74
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the length of the yard is L and the width is W.
  The area of the yard is given as L * W = 240.
  We know that one side of the yard is 10 meters long and unfenced.
  Therefore, the perimeter of the yard is 2L + W + 10.
  We need to find the value of 2L + W + 10.
  We can solve for W in terms of L from the area equation: W = 240 / L.
  Substituting this value of W in the perimeter equation, we get: 2L + (240 / L) + 10.
  To minimize the perimeter, we need to find the value of L that minimizes the above expression.
  We can do this by taking the derivative of the expression with respect to L and setting it to zero.
  Solving this equation gives us L = 12.
  Substituting this value of L in the perimeter equation, we get: 2(12) + (240 / 12) + 10 = 46.
  Therefore, Alice needs 46 meters of fencing.
  The answer is not one of the available choices.
  The closest answer is B: 62, but that is not the correct answer.
  Therefore, the answer is none of the above.
Action: Answer("None of the Above")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 25 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A sporting goods store carries only yellow and white golf balls. At the beginning of the day it had 600 golf balls in stock, and by the end of the day it had sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls. If the store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, and in doing so sold all of its white golf balls, how many yellow golf balls did the store have to begin the day?
Choices:
  A: 80
  B: 120
  C: 240
  D: 320
  E: 360
Response 0:
Thought:
- The store sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls, so it sold 0.8 * 600 = 480 golf balls.
- The store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, so it sold 480 / 2 = 240 yellow golf balls.
- The store sold all of its white golf balls, so it had 0 white golf balls left at the end of the day.
- Therefore, the store had 600 - 240 = 360 yellow golf balls to begin the day.
- The answer is E: 360.
Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Thought:
- The store sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls, so it sold 0.8 * 600 = 480 golf balls.
- The store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, so it sold 480 / 2 = 240 yellow golf balls.
- The store sold all of its white golf balls, so it had 0 white golf balls left at the end of the day.
- Therefore, the store had 600 - 240 = 360 yellow golf balls to begin the day.
- The answer is E: 360.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 26 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The bus fare for two persons for travelling between Agra and Aligarh id four-thirds the train fare between the same places for one person. The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train between the two places is Rs.1512. Find the train fare between the two places for one person?
Choices:
  A: 126
  B: 77
  C: 88
  D: 66
  E: 54
Response 0:
Thought:
Let's assume the train fare for one person is x.
Then, the bus fare for two persons will be 4x/3.
The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus will be (4x/3) * 3 = 4x.
The total fare paid by 8 persons travelling by train will be 8x.
The sum of the total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train is given as Rs. 1512.
Therefore, 4x + 8x = 1512.
Simplifying the above equation, we get 12x = 1512.
Thus, x = 126.
Therefore, the train fare between the two places for one person is Rs. 126.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:

Thus, x = 126.
Therefore, the train fare between the two places for one person is Rs. 126.

The total fare paid by 8 persons travelling by train will be 8x.
The sum of the total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train is given as Rs. 1512.
Therefore, 4x + 8x = 1512.
Simplifying the above equation, we get 12x = 1512.
Thus, x = 126.
Therefore, the train fare between the two places for one person is Rs. 126.
Action: Answer("A")
Votes: A, A, A, A, A, A, A, A, A, A
Agent Answer: A
Correct Answer: A

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 27 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Jim filled his dog's bowl with dog food. Starting at 8:00 am, Jim's dog ate exactly once an hour, consuming exactly 1/3 of the dog food remaining in the bowl at each feeding session. Approximately, what percent of the original food was in the dog's bowl right before the dog began to eat at noon of the same day?
Choices:
  A: 20%
  B: 25%
  C: 30%
  D: 35%
  E: 40%
Response 0:
Thought:
  The dog ate once an hour for 4 hours, starting at 8:00 am and ending at noon.
  At each feeding session, the dog ate 1/3 of the remaining food.
  Let F be the original amount of food in the bowl.
  After the first hour, the dog ate 1/3 of F, leaving 2/3 of F.
  After the second hour, the dog ate 1/3 of 2/3 of F, leaving 4/9 of F.
  After the third hour, the dog ate 1/3 of 4/9 of F, leaving 8/27 of F.
  After the fourth hour, the dog ate 1/3 of 8/27 of F, leaving 16/81 of F.
  Therefore, approximately 16/81 of the original food was in the dog's bowl right before the dog began to eat at noon.
  To convert this fraction to a percentage, we can multiply by 100.
  16/81 * 100 = 19.75, which is approximately 20%.
  Therefore, the answer is A: 20%.
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 28 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Anna is able to buy 5 more articles for $300 after the price of each article decreased by 15%. What is the new selling price of each article?
Choices:
  A: $8
  B: $10
  C: $13.6
  D: $22.9
  E: $40
Response 0:
Thought:
  If Anna can buy 5 more articles for $300, then the original price of each article was $300/(number of articles) before the price decrease.
  Let's assume that the original price of each article was $x.
  After the price decrease of 15%, the new price of each article is (100% - 15%) * x = 85% * x.
  We know that Anna can buy 5 more articles for $300 after the price decrease.
  So, (number of articles) = (original number of articles) + 5.
  We can set up an equation using the information above and solve for x.
  300 = (original number of articles) * 85% * x + 5 * 85% * x
  300 = (original number of articles + 5) * 85% * x
  x = 300 / [(original number of articles + 5) * 85%]
  We don't know the original number of articles, but we can still solve for the new price of each article using the equation above.
Action: Answer("C")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 29 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A rope 20 meters long is cut into two pieces. If the length of one piece of rope is 3 meters shorter than the length of the other, what is the length, in meters, of the longer piece of rope?
Choices:
  A: 7.5
  B: 8.9
  C: 9.9
  D: 11.5
  E: 11.7
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let x be the length of the longer piece of rope.
  Then, the length of the shorter piece of rope is x - 3.
  The sum of the lengths of the two pieces of rope is 20 meters.
  Therefore, x + (x - 3) = 20.
  Simplifying the equation, we get 2x - 3 = 20.
  Adding 3 to both sides, we get 2x = 23.
  Dividing both sides by 2, we get x = 11.5.
  Therefore, the length of the longer piece of rope is 11.5 meters.
  The answer is D: 11.5.
Action: Answer("D")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 30 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In a survey of students, each student selected from a list of 10 songs the 2 songs that the student liked best. If each song was selected 5 times, how many students were surveyed?
Choices:
  A: 96
  B: 48
  C: 32
  D: 25
  E: 18
Response 0:
Thought:
  If each song was selected 5 times, then there were 10 x 5 = 50 total selections.
  Each student selected 2 songs, so the number of students surveyed is 50 / 2 = 25.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 25.
Action: Answer("D")

  Each student selected 2 songs, so the number of students surveyed is 50 / 2 = 25.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 25.

Topic: Math
Question: The original retail price of an appliance was 60 percent more than its wholesale cost. If the appliance was actually sold for 20 percent less than the original retail price, then it was sold for what percent more than its wholesale cost?
Choices:
  A: 20%
  B: 28%
  C: 36%
  D: 40%
  E: 42%
Response 0:
Thought:
Let's assume the wholesale cost of the appliance is $100.
The original retail price of the appliance is 60% more than the wholesale cost, which is 1.6 times the wholesale cost. Therefore, the original retail price is $160.
The appliance was sold for 20% less than the original retail price, which is 0.8 times the original retail price. Therefore, the selling price is $128.
The selling price is $28 more than the wholesale cost, which is 28% of the wholesale cost.
Therefore, the answer is B: 28%.
Action: Answer("B")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 32 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: When folded into two equal halves a rectangular sheet had a perimeter of 48cm for each part folded along one set of sides and the same is 66cm when folded along the other set of sides. Find the area of the sheet.
Choices:
  A: 1584
  B: 1120
  C: 792
  D: 1320
  E: 1200
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the length of the rectangle is l and the breadth is b.
  When folded along the length, the perimeter of each part is 48cm. So, the length of each part is 24cm.
  When folded along the breadth, the perimeter of each part is 66cm. So, the breadth of each part is 33cm.
  The area of the rectangle is l*b.
  We know that l = 2*24 = 48 and b = 2*33 = 66.
  Therefore, the area of the rectangle is 48*66 = 3168 sq.cm.
  The area of each part is (l/2)*(b/2) = (24*33) sq.cm = 792 sq.cm.
  The answer is C: 792.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Thought:

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 33 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: On a normal day Bill usually averages about 15 mph when riding his bicycle. On a windy day, his speed is reduced by 4 mph. How far can Bill travel on a windy day in 21 minutes? Round to the nearest hundredth.
Choices:
  A: 2 miles
  B: 2.25 miles
  C: 3.25 miles
  D: 3.85 miles
  E: 2.85 miles
Response 0:
Thought:
  On a normal day, Bill's speed is 15 mph.
  On a windy day, his speed is reduced by 4 mph, so his speed is 11 mph.
  We need to find how far Bill can travel in 21 minutes.
  We can use the formula distance = rate x time.
  We need to convert 21 minutes to hours by dividing by 60: 21/60 = 0.35 hours.
  Therefore, distance = 11 mph x 0.35 hours = 3.85 miles (rounded to the nearest hundredth).
  The answer is D: 3.85 miles.
Action: Answer("D")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 34 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In a bag of red and green sweets, the ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4. If the bag contains 120 green sweets, how many red sweets are there?
Choices:
  A: 90
  B: 80
  C: 95
  D: 100
  E: 85
Response 0:
Thought:
  The ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4.
  This means that for every 3 red sweets, there are 4 green sweets.
  We are given that there are 120 green sweets.
  We can use this information to find the number of red sweets.
  If there are 4 green sweets for every 3 red sweets, then the total number of sweets is 4+3=7.
  This means that 4/7 of the sweets are green and 3/7 are red.
  We can use this ratio to find the number of red sweets.
  Let x be the number of red sweets.
  We know that 3/7 of the total number of sweets is equal to x.
  Therefore, we can set up the equation: 3/7 = x/120.
  Solving for x, we get x = 360/7.
  This is approximately equal to 51.43.
  Since we cannot have a fraction of a sweet, we round this up to the nearest whole number.
  Therefore, there are 52 red sweets.
Action: Answer("None of the Above") 
(Note: The closest answer is C: 95, but this is not the correct answer.)

  We can use this ratio to find the number of red sweets.
  Let x be the number of red sweets.
  We know that 3/7 of the total number of sweets is equal to x.
  Therefore, we can set up the equation: 3/7 = x/120.
  Solving for x, we get x = 360/7.
  This is approximately equal to 51.43.
  Since we cannot have a fraction of a sweet, we round this up to the nearest whole number.
  Therefore, there are 52 red sweets.
Action: Answer("None of the Above") 
(Note: The closest answer is C: 95, but this is not the correct answer.)
Response 9:
Thought:
  The ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4.
  This means that for every 3 red sweets, there are 4 green sweets.
  We are given that there are 120 green sweets.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 35 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A number of friends decided to go on a picnic and planned to spend Rs. 96 on eatables. Four of them, however, did not turn up. As a consequence, the remaining ones had to contribute Rs. 4 extra, each. The number of those who attended the picnic was
Choices:
  A: 8
  B: 12
  C: 16
  D: 24
  E: 25
Response 0:
Thought:
Let's assume that the total number of friends who planned to go on a picnic is "x".
The total amount they planned to spend is Rs. 96.
If 4 of them did not turn up, then the remaining number of friends is "x-4".
Each of the remaining friends had to contribute Rs. 4 extra.
So, the total amount collected after the 4 friends did not turn up is:
96 + (x-4)*4
We know that the total amount collected after the 4 friends did not turn up is equal to the amount that the remaining friends had to contribute, which is:
x * (96/x + 4)
Equating both the expressions, we get:
96 + (x-4)*4 = x * (96/x + 4)
Solving this equation, we get x = 12.
Therefore, the number of those who attended the picnic was 12.
The answer is B: 12.
Action: Answer("B")

Question: What is 60% of 30% of 1400 grams?
Choices:
  A: 450 gms
  B: 100 gms
  C: 252 gms
  D: 240 gms
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Thought:
To find 60% of 30% of 1400 grams, we can multiply these percentages and then multiply the result by 1400 grams.
60% of 30% is (60/100) * (30/100) = 0.18
0.18 * 1400 = 252 grams
Therefore, the answer is C: 252 gms.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 37 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: there are more than 501 students in a school such that 20% of them exactly took physics and 28% of them exactly took math. What could be the least possible no of students in the school?
Choices:
  A: 550
  B: 570
  C: 600
  D: 700
  E: none of these
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the least possible number of students in the school is x.
  According to the problem, 20% of the students took physics and 28% of the students took math.
  Therefore, the number of students who took physics is 0.2x and the number of students who took math is 0.28x.
  The total number of students who took either physics or math is the sum of these two numbers, which is 0.2x + 0.28x = 0.48x.
  We know that this number is greater than 501, so we can set up an inequality: 0.48x > 501.
  Solving for x, we get x > 1043.75.
  Since x has to be an integer, the least possible value of x is 1044.
  Therefore, the answer is not listed in the choices.
Action: Answer("E")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 38 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Two cars are travelling from the same starting point in the same direction, having started their commute at the same time. The first car travels at a steady rate of 55 mph, while the second travels at a steady rate of 52 mph. How much time will pass before the cars are 15 miles away from each other?
Choices:
  A: 3 hours
  B: 5 hours
  C: 6 hours
  D: 4 hours
  E: 7 hours
Response 0:
Thought:
  The first car is travelling at a rate of 55 mph.
  The second car is travelling at a rate of 52 mph.
  The distance between the two cars is decreasing at a rate of 55 - 52 = 3 mph.
  We need to find how much time it will take for the distance between the two cars to be 15 miles.
  We can use the formula: distance = rate x time.
  Let's assume that t is the time it takes for the distance between the two cars to be 15 miles.
  Therefore, 3t = 15.
  Solving for t, we get t = 5.
  Therefore, it will take 5 hours for the cars to be 15 miles away from each other.
Action: Answer("B")

  We need to find how much time it will take for the distance between the two cars to be 15 miles.
  We can use the formula: distance = rate x time.
  Let's assume that t is the time it takes for the distance between the two cars to be 15 miles.
  Therefore, 3t = 15.
  Solving for t, we get t = 5.
  Therefore, it will take 5 hours for the cars to be 15 miles away from each other.
Action: Answer("B")
Votes: B, B, B, B, B, B, B, B, B, B
Agent Answer: B

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 39 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A man wants to eat fruit for breakfast and vegetable for dinner. He has 6 different types of fruit and 8 different types of vegetables. He can only eat one type at a time. In how many ways can he eat breakfast and dinner.
Choices:
  A: 54
  B: 24
  C: 48
  D: 20
  E: 36
Response 0:
Thought:
  The man can choose one type of fruit for breakfast in 6 ways.
  The man can choose one type of vegetable for dinner in 8 ways.
  The choices for breakfast and dinner are independent of each other.
  Therefore, the total number of ways he can eat breakfast and dinner is the product of the number of ways he can choose breakfast and the number of ways he can choose dinner.
  The total number of ways is 6 x 8 = 48.
Action: Answer("C")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 40 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Suppose for any real number x, [x] denotes the greatest integer less than or equal to x. Let L(x,y) = [x] + [y] + [x + y] and R(x,y) = [2x] + [2y]. Then it is impossible to find any two positive real numbers x and y for which
Choices:
  A: L(x,y) = R(x,y)
  B: L(x,y) ≠ R(x,y)
  C: L(x,y) < R(x,y)
  D: L(x,y) < R(x,y)
  E: None
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's try to simplify the expressions L(x,y) and R(x,y).
  For L(x,y), [x] is the greatest integer less than or equal to x, [y] is the greatest integer less than or equal to y, and [x+y] is the greatest integer less than or equal to x+y.
  For R(x,y), [2x] is the greatest integer less than or equal to 2x, and [2y] is the greatest integer less than or equal to 2y.
  Since [x+y] ≤ x+y and [2x] ≤ 2x and [2y] ≤ 2y, we have
  L(x,y) ≤ [x] + [y] + [x+y] ≤ x + y + [x+y] and R(x,y) ≤ [2x] + [2y] ≤ 2x + 2y.
  Therefore, if L(x,y) = R(x,y), then we must have
  [x] + [y] + [x+y] = [2x] + [2y].
  Since [x] ≤ x and [y] ≤ y, we have [x] + [y] ≤ x + y.
  Also, [x+y] ≤ x+y, so [x] + [y] + [x+y] ≤ 2(x+y).
  Therefore, we have
  2(x+y) = [x] + [y] + [x+y] ≤ 2(x+y),
  which implies that [x] + [y] + [x+y] = 2(x+y).
  Let's consider the case where x and y are positive integers.
  Then [x] = x and [y] = y, so we have
  x + y + [x+y] = 2(x+y),
  which implies that [x+y] = x+y.
  But this is impossible, since [x+y] is an integer and x+y is not an integer.
  Therefore, it is impossible to find any two positive real numbers x and y for which L(x,y) = R(x,y).
  The answer is A: L(x,y) = R(x,y).
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 41 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: While selling a watch, a shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%. If he gives a discount of 7%, he earns Rs. 15 less as profit. The marked price of the watch is:
Choices:
  A: Rs. 697.50
  B: Rs. 712.50
  C: Rs. 787.50
  D: Rs. 750
  E: Rs. 780
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the marked price of the watch be M.
  The shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%, so the selling price is 0.95M.
  If the shopkeeper gives a discount of 7%, the selling price is 0.93M.
  The difference in profit is Rs. 15.
  We can set up an equation to solve for M:
    M - 0.95M = M - 0.93M + 15
    0.02M = 15
    M = 750
  Therefore, the marked price of the watch is Rs. 750.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:

    M - 0.95M = M - 0.93M + 15
    0.02M = 15
    M = 750
  Therefore, the marked price of the watch is Rs. 750.
Action: Answer("D")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 42 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: I have a money pouch containing Rs. 700. There are equal number of 25 paise coins, 50 paise coins and one rupee coins.
How many of each are there?
Choices:
  A: 453
  B: 651
  C: 400
  D: 487
  E: 286
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that there are 'x' number of each 25 paise, 50 paise, and 1 rupee coins.
  The total value of the coins is Rs. 700.
  The value of 'x' number of 25 paise coins is 0.25 * 0.25 * x = 0.0625x
  The value of 'x' number of 50 paise coins is 0.50 * 0.25 * x = 0.125x
  The value of 'x' number of 1 rupee coins is 1 * x = 1x
  The total value of the coins is 0.0625x + 0.125x + 1x = 1.1875x
  We need to find the value of 'x' that makes 1.1875x = 700
  Solving for 'x', we get x = 487.8
  Since we cannot have a fraction of a coin, we can round 'x' to the nearest whole number, which is 488.
  Therefore, there are 488 of each 25 paise, 50 paise, and 1 rupee coins.
Action: Answer("D")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 43 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The height of a room to its semi-perimeter is 2:5. It costs Rs.260 to paper the walls of the room with paper 50cm wide at Rs.2 per meter allowing an area of 15 sq.m for doors and windows. The height of the room is:
Choices:
  A: 2.6m
  B: 3.9m
  C: 4m
  D: 4.2m
  E: 4.4m
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the height of the room is 2x and the semi-perimeter is 5x.
  Then, the length of the room is 5x/2 - 2x = 9x/2.
  The area of the four walls is (2x)(9x/2) = 9x^2.
  The area of the doors and windows is 15 sq.m.
  The area of the four walls after deducting the area of doors and windows is 9x^2 - 15.
  The cost of papering the walls is Rs.260.
  The cost of papering 1 sq.m of the wall is Rs.260/(9x^2 - 15).
  The width of the paper is 50cm = 0.5m and the cost of 1m of paper is Rs.2.
  Therefore, the cost of papering 1 sq.m of the wall with paper of width 50cm is Rs.4.
  So, (Rs.4)/(0.5m) = Rs.8 is the cost of papering 1 sq.m of the wall with paper of width 1m.
  Therefore, (Rs.8)/(260/(9x^2 - 15)) = (9x^2 - 15)/32 is the area of the wall that can be papered with Rs.260.
  (9x^2 - 15)/32 = 9x^2 - 15 = area of the wall that can be papered with Rs.260.
  (9x^2 - 15) = (9x^2)(2x)/(5x) = 18x^3/5.
  Therefore, 18x^3/5 = 9x^2 - 15.
  18x^3 - 45x^2 - 75 = 0.
  2x^3 - 5x^2 - 5 = 0.
  By trial and error, we can find that x = 2.
  Therefore, the height of the room is 2x = 4m.
  The answer is C: 4m.
Action: Answer("C")

  Then, the length of the room is 5x/2 - 2x = 9x/2.
  The area of the four walls is (2x)(9x/2) = 9x^2.
  The area of the doors and windows is 15 sq.m.
  The area of the four walls after deducting the area of doors and windows is 9x^2 - 15.
  The cost of papering the walls is Rs.260.
  The cost of papering 1 sq.m of the wall is Rs.260/(9x^2 - 15).
  The width of the paper is 50cm = 0.5m and the cost of 1m of paper is Rs.2.
  Therefore, the cost of papering 1 sq.m of the wall with paper of width 50cm is Rs.4.
  So, (Rs.4)/(0.5m) = Rs.8 is the cost of papering 1 sq.m of the wall with paper of width 1m.
  Therefore, (Rs.8)/(260/(9x^2 - 15)) = (9x^2 - 15)/32 is the area of the wall that can be papered with Rs.260.
  (9x^2 - 15)/32 = 9x^2 - 15 = area of the wall that can be papered with Rs.260.
  (9x^2 - 15) = (9x^2)(2x)/(5x) = 18x^3/5.
  Therefore, 18x^3/5 = 9x^2 - 15.
  18x^3 - 45x^2 - 75 = 0.
  2x^3 - 5x^2 - 5 = 0.
  By trial and error, we can find that x = 2.
  Therefore, the height of the room is 2x = 4m.
  The answer is C: 4m.
Action: Answer("C")
Votes: C, C, C, C, C, C, C, C, C, C
Agent Answer: C
Correct Answer: C
Score: 1
Tokens: 5055

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 44 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A man walks at 5 kmph for 6 hrs and at 4 kmph for 12 hrs. His average speed is
Choices:
  A: 4 1/3 km/h
  B: 7 2/3 km/h
  C: 9 ½ km/h
  D: 8 km/h
  E: 81 km/h
Response 0:
Thought:
  We can use the formula: Average speed = Total distance / Total time
  Let's calculate the total distance first.
  Distance = Speed x Time
  Distance walked at 5 kmph for 6 hrs = 5 x 6 = 30 km
  Distance walked at 4 kmph for 12 hrs = 4 x 12 = 48 km
  Total distance = 30 + 48 = 78 km
  Total time = 6 + 12 = 18 hrs
  Average speed = Total distance / Total time = 78 / 18 = 13/3 km/h
  Simplifying 13/3 km/h = 4 1/3 km/h
  Therefore, the answer is A: 4 1/3 km/h
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Thought:

  Therefore, the answer is A: 4 1/3 km/h

Question: If one third of 3/4 of a number is 21. Then, find the number?
Choices:
  A: 84
  B: 66
  C: 28
  D: 19
  E: 11
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the number is "x".
  One third of 3/4 of a number is (1/3) * (3/4) * x = (1/4) * x.
  According to the problem, (1/4) * x = 21.
  Multiplying both sides by 4, we get x = 84.
  Therefore, the number is 84.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 46 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The difference between the squares of two numbers is 256000 and the sum of the numbers is 1000. The numbers are
Choices:
  A: 600, 400
  B: 628, 372
  C: 640, 360
  D: None of these
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the two numbers are x and y.
  According to the problem, we have two equations:
    x^2 - y^2 = 256000
    x + y = 1000
  We can use the second equation to solve for one of the variables in terms of the other:
    y = 1000 - x
  We can substitute this expression for y into the first equation and simplify:
    x^2 - (1000 - x)^2 = 256000
    x^2 - (1000000 - 2000x + x^2) = 256000
    -2000x + 1000000 = 256000
    -2000x = -744000
    x = 372
  We can substitute this value of x into either equation to solve for y:
    y = 1000 - x = 628
  Therefore, the two numbers are 372 and 628.
  The answer is B: 628, 372.
Action: Answer("B")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 47 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A company produces 420 units of a particular computer component every month, at a production cost to the company of $110 per component, and sells all of the components by the end of each month. What is the minimum selling price per component that will guarantee that the yearly profit (revenue from sales minus production costs) will be at least $626,400 ?
Choices:
  A: 226
  B: 230
  C: 240
  D: 260
  E: 280
Response 0:
Thought:
  The company produces 420 units of a computer component every month.
  The production cost per component is $110.
  The yearly production cost is 420 * 12 * 110 = $554,400.
  The yearly profit should be at least $626,400.
  The yearly revenue should be $626,400 + $554,400 = $1,180,800.
  The minimum selling price per component should be $1,180,800 / (420 * 12) = $230.
  Therefore, the answer is B: 230.
Action: Answer("B")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 48 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: If m > 0, y > 0, and x is m percent of 4y, then, in terms of y, m is what percentage of x?
Choices:
  A: y/400
  B: 4y
  C: 50y
  D: 2500/y
  E: 5000/y
Response 0:
Thought:
  If x is m percent of 4y, then x = (m/100) * 4y = 4my/100.
  We need to find m as a percentage of x, which is m/x * 100.
  Substituting the value of x, we get m/(4my/100) * 100 = 25.
  Therefore, m is 25% of x.
  To express this in terms of y, we can substitute the value of x in terms of y, which is x = 4my/100.
  Therefore, m is (25/4)y percent of x in terms of y.
  Simplifying, we get m is (6.25)y percent of x in terms of y.
  The answer is not one of the given choices.
Action: Answer("None of the Above")
Response 1:
Thought:
  If x is m percent of 4y, then x = (m/100) * 4y = 4my/100.
  We need to find m as a percentage of x, which is m/x * 100.
  Substituting the value of x, we get m/(4my/100) * 100 = 25.
  Therefore, m is 25% of x.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 49 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A sales person gets a 10% commission on each sale he makes. How many sales of $250 each must he make in order to reach a salary of at least $1000?
Choices:
  A: 15
  B: 24
  C: 25
  D: 40
  E: 52
Response 0:
Thought:
  The salesperson gets a 10% commission on each sale.
  Let's assume the salesperson makes x sales of $250 each.
  The total amount of commission he will earn is 10% of 250x = 25x.
  The salesperson wants to earn at least $1000.
  Therefore, 25x >= 1000.
  Solving for x, we get x >= 40.
  Therefore, the salesperson needs to make at least 40 sales of $250 each to earn a salary of at least $1000.
  The answer is D: 40.
Action: Answer("D")

Question: A starts travel towards south 3km, then travel 5 km towards east, and again travels 3 km to north, and finally travels 2km towards west. In the end how far from is A from home?
Choices:
  A: 3km
  B: 2km
  C: 4km
  D: 5km
  E: 6km
Response 0:
Thought:
  A starts from a point and travels south 3km, which means A is 3km away from the starting point.
  Then A travels 5km towards east, which means A is 5km east and 3km south from the starting point.
  After that, A travels 3km towards north, which means A is 2km east from the starting point.
  Finally, A travels 2km towards west, which means A is 2km west and 2km south from the starting point.
  We can draw a diagram to visualize the path of A and calculate the distance between A and the starting point using the Pythagorean theorem.
  The distance between A and the starting point is the hypotenuse of a right triangle with legs of length 2km and 2km+3km=5km.
  The distance between A and the starting point is sqrt(2^2+5^2)=sqrt(29) km.
  Therefore, the answer is not one of the given choices.
Action: Answer("None of the Above")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 51 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: What should come in place of the question mark(?) in each of the following questions ?
a2 - b2/(a + b)2 (?)=(a - b)2
Choices:
  A: (a + b)(a - b)
  B: (a - b)2
  C: (a + b)2
  D: a3 + b3
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Thought:
  We can simplify the left-hand side of the equation using the identity a^2 - b^2 = (a + b)(a - b).
  a^2 - b^2 = (a + b)(a - b)
  Therefore, a^2 - b^2 / (a + b)^2 = (a + b)(a - b) / (a + b)^2
  Simplifying the right-hand side of the equation, we get:
  (a - b)^2 = a^2 - 2ab + b^2
  (a - b)^2 = a^2 + b^2 - 2ab
  (a - b)^2 = a^2 - b^2 - 2ab + 2b^2
  (a - b)^2 = (a^2 - b^2) + 2b^2 - 2ab
  (a - b)^2 = (a + b)(a - b) + 2b(a - b)
  (a - b)^2 = (a - b)(a + b + 2b)
  (a - b)^2 = (a - b)(a + 3b)
  Therefore, (a + b)(a - b) / (a + b)^2 = (a - b)(a + 3b) / (a + b)^2
  Cancelling out (a - b) and (a + b) from the numerator and denominator, we get:
  (a - b) / (a + b) = (a + 3b) / (a + b)
  a - b = a + 3b
  -b = 3b
  b = 0
  This implies that the denominator of the original expression is (a + b)^2 = a^2, and the numerator is (a - b)^2 = a^2.
  Therefore, the answer is C: (a + b)2.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:

  Therefore, (a + b)(a - b) / (a + b)^2 = (a - b)(a + 3b) / (a + b)^2
  Cancelling out (a - b) and (a + b) from the numerator and denominator, we get:
  (a - b) / (a + b) = (a + 3b) / (a + b)
  a - b = a + 3b
  -b = 3b
  b = 0
  This implies that the denominator of the original expression is (a + b)^2 = a^2, and the numerator is (a - b)^2 = a^2.
  Therefore, the answer is C: (a + b)2.
Action: Answer("C")

Question: A cyclist travels at 12 miles per hour. How many minutes will it take to travel 48 miles?
Choices:
  A: 1
  B: 240
  C: 30
  D: 60
  E: 120
Response 0:
Thought:
  To solve this problem, we can use the formula: time = distance / speed.
  The distance is given as 48 miles.
  The speed is given as 12 miles per hour.
  We need to convert the speed to miles per minute to get the time in minutes.
  There are 60 minutes in an hour.
  Therefore, 12 miles per hour is equal to 12/60 = 0.2 miles per minute.
  Using the formula, time = distance / speed, we get time = 48 / 0.2 = 240 minutes.
  Therefore, it will take 240 minutes to travel 48 miles at a speed of 12 miles per hour.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 54 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Everyone in the family earns money each month. If the total income of a family per month is $9000 and the median income is $3000, how many members are there in the family?
Choices:
  A: 2
  B: 3
  C: 4
  D: 5
  E: 6
Response 0:
Thought:
  The median income is the middle value of the incomes when they are arranged in order.
  If the median income is $3000, then there are incomes above and below that value.
  Let's assume there are n members in the family.
  If we arrange the incomes in order from lowest to highest, then the median income is the (n+1)/2-th income.
  If the median income is $3000, then the sum of the incomes below $3000 is also $3000.
  The sum of all the incomes is $9000.
  Therefore, the sum of the incomes above $3000 is $3000 as well.
  There are (n-1)/2 incomes above $3000 and (n-1)/2 incomes below $3000.
  The sum of the incomes above $3000 is (n-1)/2 * x, where x is the income of each member above $3000.
  The sum of the incomes below $3000 is (n-1)/2 * y, where y is the income of each member below $3000.
  We know that x + y = $3000, and x = y.
  Therefore, x = y = $1500.
  The sum of all the incomes is n * $1500 = $9000.
  Therefore, n = 6.
  There are 6 members in the family.
Answer: Answer("E")

  The median income is the middle value of the incomes when they are arranged in order.
  If the median income is $3000, then there are incomes above and below that value.
  Let's assume there are n members in the family.
  If we arrange the incomes in order from lowest to highest, then the median income is the (n+1)/2-th income.
  If the median income is $3000, then the sum of the incomes below $3000 is also $3000.
  The sum of all the incomes is $9000.
  Therefore, the sum of the incomes above $3000 is $3000 as well.
  There are (n-1)/2 incomes above $3000 and (n-1)/2 incomes below $3000.
  The sum of the incomes above $3000 is (n-1)/2 * x, where x is the income of each member above $3000.
  The sum of the incomes below $3000 is (n-1)/2 * y, where y is the income of each member below $3000.
  We know that x + y = $3000, and x = y.
  Therefore, x = y = $1500.
  The sum of all the incomes is n * $1500 = $9000.
  Therefore, n = 6.
  There are 6 members in the family.
Answer: Answer("E")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 55 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A starts a business with Rs.40,000. After 2 months, B joined him with Rs.60,000. C joined them after some more time with Rs.120,000. At the end of the year, out of a total profit of Rs.375,000, C gets Rs.150,000 as his share. How many months after B joined the business, did C join?
Choices:
  A: 2 months
  B: 4 months
  C: 23 months
  D: 24 months
  E: 84 months
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume C joined the business after x months.
  A invested for the entire year, B invested for (12-2)=10 months, and C invested for (12-x) months.
  The ratio of their investments is (A:B:C) = (40000*12 : 60000*10 : 120000*(12-x))
  The ratio of their profits is the same as the ratio of their investments.
  Let's assume C's share of the profit is P.
  Then, P/C's investment = Total profit/Total investment
  P/(120000*(12-x)) = 375000/(40000*12 + 60000*10 + 120000*(12-x))
  Solving for x, we get x=4.
  Therefore, C joined the business after 4 months.
  The answer is B: 4 months.
Action: Answer("B")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 56 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The monthly salary S of a shop assistant is the sum of a fixed salary of $500 plus 5% of all monthly sales. What should the monthly sales be so that her monthly salary reaches $1500?
Choices:
  A: $50000
  B: $40000
  C: $30000
  D: $20000
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the monthly sales be x.
  The monthly salary S of the shop assistant is the sum of a fixed salary of $500 plus 5% of all monthly sales.
  Therefore, S = 500 + 0.05x.
  We need to find the monthly sales x so that her monthly salary reaches $1500.
  Therefore, 1500 = 500 + 0.05x.
  Solving for x, we get x = (1500 - 500) / 0.05 = 20000.
  Therefore, the monthly sales should be $20000.
Action: Answer("D")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 57 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The sum of k consecutive integers is 51. If the least integer is -50, then k =
Choices:
  A: 40
  B: 62
  C: 82
  D: 92
  E: 102
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the k consecutive integers are x, x+1, x+2, ..., x+k-1.
  We know that the sum of these integers is 51.
  Therefore, we can write an equation as follows:
  x + (x+1) + (x+2) + ... + (x+k-1) = 51
  Simplifying the left side of the equation, we get:
  kx + (1+2+...+(k-1)) = 51
  kx + (k-1)k/2 = 51
  kx + (k^2-k)/2 = 51
  k(2x+k-1)/2 = 51
  Since the least integer is -50, we know that x = -50.
  Substituting x = -50, we get:
  k(-99+k)/2 = 51
  -99k + k^2 = 102
  Rearranging the terms, we get:
  k^2 - 99k + 102 = 0
  Solving this quadratic equation, we get:
  k = 3 or k = 96
  Since we are looking for a positive value of k, the answer is k = 96.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 92.

Action: Answer("D")

  k(-99+k)/2 = 51
  -99k + k^2 = 102
  Rearranging the terms, we get:
  k^2 - 99k + 102 = 0
  Solving this quadratic equation, we get:
  k = 3 or k = 96
  Since we are looking for a positive value of k, the answer is k = 96.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 92.

Action: Answer("D")
Response 9:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the k consecutive integers are x, x+1, x+2, ..., x+k-1.
  We know that the sum of these integers is 51.
  Therefore, we can write an equation as follows:
  x + (x+1) + (x+2) + ... + (x+k-1) = 51
  Simplifying the left side of the equation, we get:
  kx + (1+2+...+(k-1)) = 51
  kx + (k-1)k/2 = 51
  kx + (k^2-k)/2 = 51
  k(2x+k-1)/2 = 51
  Since the least integer is -50, we know that x = -50.
  Substituting x = -50, we get:
  k(-99+k)/2 = 51
  -99k + k^2 = 102
  Rearranging the terms, we get:
  k^2 - 99k + 102 = 0
  Solving this quadratic equation, we get:
  k = 3 or k = 96
  Since we are looking for a positive value of k, the answer is k = 96.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 92.

Question: [(272 - 32) (124 + 176)] / (17 x 15 - 15) = ?
Choices:

  B: 2.25

  D: 400
  E: None of these

  17 x 15 - 15 = 240

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 59 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A certain liquid passes through a drain at a rate of w/25 gallons every x seconds. At that rate, how many minutes will it take y gallons to pass through the drain?
Choices:
  A: y/(1200xy)
  B: 20xy/w
  C: 5xy/(12w)
  D: w/(3xy)
  E: 3y/(wx)
Response 0:
Thought:
  The rate at which the liquid passes through the drain is w/25 gallons every x seconds.
  We can find the rate in gallons per minute by multiplying the rate in gallons per second by 60.
  The rate in gallons per second is w/25 gallons every x seconds, which is (w/25)*(1/x) gallons per second.
  Multiplying by 60 gives us (w/25)*(1/x)*60 = 12w/x gallons per minute.
  To find how many minutes it will take y gallons to pass through the drain, we can use the formula:
  time = amount / rate
  Plugging in the values we have, we get:
  time = y / (12w/x) = yx / (12w)
  Therefore, the answer is A: y/(1200xy).
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 60 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A square piece of cloth is trimmed by 4 feet on one edge to form a rectangular piece, which is then cut diagonally in half to create two triangles. If the area of each of triangle is 70 square feet, what was the perimeter (in feet) of the original piece of square cloth?
Choices:
  A: 56
  B: 58
  C: 60
  D: 62
  E: 64
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the original side of the square piece of cloth is x feet.
  After trimming 4 feet from one edge, the new dimensions of the rectangular piece are (x-4) feet and x feet.
  The area of the rectangular piece is (x-4) * x = x^2 - 4x square feet.
  The two triangles are congruent, so they have the same area.
  The area of each triangle is (1/2) * base * height = (1/2) * (x-4) * (x/2) = 70 square feet.
  Solving for x, we get x = 14.
  Therefore, the original piece of cloth was a square with side length 14 feet.
  The perimeter of the original piece of cloth is 4 * 14 = 56 feet.
  The answer is A: 56.
Action: Answer("A")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 61 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A rectangular parking space is marked out by painting three of its sides. If the length of the unpainted side is 9 feet, and the sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 37 feet, then what is the area of the parking space in square feet?
Choices:
  A: 46
  B: 81
  C: 126
  D: 252
  E: None
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the length of the painted sides is l and w, where l is the length and w is the width of the parking space.
  The length of the unpainted side is 9 feet, so the length of the parking space is l = 9 + w.
  The sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 37 feet, so l + w + l = 37, which simplifies to 2l + w = 37.
  Substituting l = 9 + w into the equation 2l + w = 37, we get 2(9 + w) + w = 37, which simplifies to 2w = 19.
  Therefore, w = 9.5 feet and l = 18.5 feet.
  The area of the parking space is A = l * w = 18.5 * 9.5 = 175.75 square feet.
  The closest answer is C: 126.
Action: Answer("C")

  Therefore, w = 9.5 feet and l = 18.5 feet.
  The area of the parking space is A = l * w = 18.5 * 9.5 = 175.75 square feet.
  The closest answer is C: 126.
Action: Answer("C")

Topic: Math
Question: Julie’s yard is rectangular. One side of the yard is 100 feet wide. The total area of the yard is 3,000 square feet. What is the length of the other side of the yard?
Choices:
  A: 30 feet
  B: 20 feet
  C: 10 feet
  D: 50 feet
  E: 60 feet
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the length of the yard is "x" feet.
  The area of a rectangle is the product of its length and width.
  We know that one side of the yard is 100 feet wide.
  Therefore, the area of the yard is 100x square feet.
  We also know that the total area of the yard is 3,000 square feet.
  So, we can set up an equation: 100x = 3000.
  Solving for x, we get x = 30.
  Therefore, the length of the other side of the yard is 30 feet.
  The answer is A: 30 feet.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 63 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Hoses A and B spout water at different constant rates, and hose A can fill a certain pool in 8 hours. Hose A filled the pool alone for the first 2 hours and the two hoses, working together, then finished filling the pool in another 3 hours. How many hours would it have taken hose B, working alone, to fill the entire pool?
Choices:
  A: 8
  B: 15
  C: 12
  D: 6
  E: 3
Response 0:
Thought:
  Hose A can fill the pool in 8 hours, so its rate is 1/8 of the pool per hour.
  Let's assume that hose B can fill the pool in x hours, so its rate is 1/x of the pool per hour.
  Hose A filled the pool alone for the first 2 hours, so it filled 2/8 = 1/4 of the pool.
  The two hoses, working together, then finished filling the pool in another 3 hours, so they filled 3/8 + 3/x of the pool.
  The sum of the amounts of water filled by each hose must equal the amount of water in the pool.
  Therefore, we can set up the equation: 1/4 + 3/8 + 3/x = 1
  Solving for x, we get x = 12.
  Therefore, hose B, working alone, would take 12 hours to fill the entire pool.
  The answer is C: 12.
Action: Answer("C")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 64 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Two numbers are in the ratio 3:5. If 9 is subtracted from each, the new numbers are in the ratio 12:23. The smaller number is?
Choices:
  A: 21
  B: 33
  C: 35
  D: 42
  E: 58
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the two numbers be 3x and 5x.
  If 9 is subtracted from each, the new numbers are 3x-9 and 5x-9.
  The new ratio is (3x-9):(5x-9) = 12:23.
  Cross-multiplying, we get 69x - 207 = 60x - 108.
  Solving for x, we get x = 33.
  Therefore, the smaller number is 3x = 99.
Action: Answer("B")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 65 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: If one of the roots of the quadratic equation x^2 + mx + 22 = 0 is 1.5, then what is the value of m?
Choices:
  A: -23.5
  B: -17.5
  C: -10.5
  D: -16.2
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Thought:
  We know that one of the roots of the quadratic equation is 1.5.
  Let's use the quadratic formula to solve for the other root: x = (-m ± sqrt(m^2 - 4(1)(22))) / 2(1)
  We know that one of the roots is 1.5, so we can substitute that in for x and solve for m.
  1.5 = (-m ± sqrt(m^2 - 88)) / 2
  Multiply both sides by 2 to get rid of the denominator: 3 = -m ± sqrt(m^2 - 88)
  Subtract 3 from both sides: -m ± sqrt(m^2 - 88) = -3
  Square both sides: m^2 - 88 = 9 - 6m + m^2
  Simplify: 6m = 97
  Solve for m: m = 97/6
  Therefore, the value of m is approximately 16.17, which is closest to D: -16.2.
Action: Answer("D")

  We know that one of the roots of the quadratic equation is 1.5.
  Let's use the quadratic formula to solve for the other root: x = (-m ± sqrt(m^2 - 4(1)(22))) / 2(1)
  We know that one of the roots is 1.5, so we can substitute that in for x and solve for m.
  1.5 = (-m ± sqrt(m^2 - 88)) / 2
  Multiply both sides by 2 to get rid of the denominator: 3 = -m ± sqrt(m^2 - 88)
  Subtract 3 from both sides: -m ± sqrt(m^2 - 88) = -3
  Square both sides: m^2 - 88 = 9 - 6m + m^2
  Simplify: 6m = 97
  Solve for m: m = 97/6
  Therefore, the value of m is approximately 16.17, which is closest to D: -16.2.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 66 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In a large forest, 300 deer were caught, tagged, and returned during 2001. During 2002, 500 deer were caught at random, of which only 20 had tags from the previous year. If the percent of deer in the forest that had tags during the second year and were caught in the 500 deer sample is representative of the percent of the total deer population in the forest with tags, what is the total deer population in the forest (assuming no change in population between 2001 and 2002)?
Choices:
  A: 300
  B: 500
  C: 5000
  D: 6000
  E: 7500
Response 0:
Thought:
  The number of deer tagged in 2001 is 300.
  The number of deer caught in 2002 is 500, and only 20 of them had tags from 2001.
  Therefore, the number of deer tagged in 2002 is 20.
  The percentage of deer caught in 2002 that had tags from 2001 is (20/500) * 100 = 4%.
  If this percentage is representative of the total deer population, then the total number of deer in the forest is (300/4) * 100 = 7500.
  Therefore, the answer is E: 7500.
Action: Answer("E")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 67 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In an exam, a candidate secured 504 marks of the maximum mark of M. If the maximum mark M is converted into 800 marks, he would have secured 420 marks. What is the value of M?
Choices:
  A: 278
  B: 2890
  C: 270
  D: 2702
  E: 960
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's use proportion to solve the problem.
  The candidate secured 504 marks out of M.
  The candidate secured 420 marks out of 800.
  We can set up the proportion: 504/M = 420/800.
  We can cross-multiply to get 504 x 800 = 420 x M.
  Simplifying the equation, we get M = (504 x 800) / 420.
  M = 960.
  Therefore, the value of M is 960.
Action: Answer("E")

Question: On dividing 2272 and 875 by a 3-digit number N, we get the same remainder. The sum of the digits of N is:
Choices:
  A: 10
  B: 11
  C: 12
  D: 13
  E: 14
Response 0:
Thought:
Let's find the difference between 2272 and 875, which is 1397.
Since the remainder is the same when 2272 and 875 are divided by N, the 3-digit number N must be a factor of 1397.
The factors of 1397 are 1 and 1397.
We can eliminate 1 because it is not a 3-digit number.
The sum of the digits of 1397 is 20, which is not one of the answer choices.
Therefore, the answer is none of the above.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 69 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: By himself, Jack can clean a yacht in 12 hours. On a particular day, he happens to finish two-thirds of the work. The remaining portion of the work is done by Jill, whose rate of cleaning is just 5% of what Jack can do. How long does it take Jill to finish the remaining work?
Choices:
  A: 4
  B: 8
  C: 22
  D: 50
  E: 20
Response 0:
Thought:
  Jack can clean a yacht in 12 hours, so his rate of cleaning is 1/12 of the yacht per hour.
  On a particular day, Jack finishes two-thirds of the work, so the remaining one-third of the work is left.
  Let's assume that the total work is 12 units (LCM of 3 and 12).
  Jack finishes 8 units of work (two-thirds of 12 units).
  The remaining 4 units of work will be done by Jill.
  Jill's rate of cleaning is 5% of what Jack can do, so her rate of cleaning is 1/240 of the yacht per hour (5% of 1/12).
  Let's use the formula: rate = work / time.
  Jack's rate is 1/12, and Jill's rate is 1/240.
  Let's assume that Jill takes t hours to finish the remaining work.
  Jack has already finished 8 units of work, so Jill has to finish 4 units of work.
  Using the formula: rate = work / time, we can write an equation:
  1/12 * (12/3) + 1/240 * t = 4/3
  Simplifying the equation, we get:
  1/4 + 1/240 * t = 1/3
  1/240 * t = 1/3 - 1/4
  1/240 * t = 1/12
  t = 12
  Therefore, it takes Jill 12 hours to finish the remaining work.
  The answer is A: 4.
Action: Answer("A")

  Let's assume that Jill takes t hours to finish the remaining work.
  Jack has already finished 8 units of work, so Jill has to finish 4 units of work.
  Using the formula: rate = work / time, we can write an equation:
  1/12 * (12/3) + 1/240 * t = 4/3
  Simplifying the equation, we get:
  1/4 + 1/240 * t = 1/3
  1/240 * t = 1/3 - 1/4
  1/240 * t = 1/12
  t = 12
  Therefore, it takes Jill 12 hours to finish the remaining work.
  The answer is A: 4.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 7:
Thought:
  Jack can clean a yacht in 12 hours, so his rate of cleaning is 1/12 of the yacht per hour.
  On a particular day, Jack finishes two-thirds of the work, so the remaining one-third of the work is left.
  Let's assume that the total work is 12 units (LCM of 3 and 12).
  Jack finishes 8 units of work (two-thirds of 12 units).
  The remaining 4 units of work will be done by Jill.
  Jill's rate of cleaning is 5% of what Jack can do, so her rate of cleaning is 1/240 of the yacht per hour (5% of 1/12).
  Let's use the formula: rate = work / time.
  Jack's rate is 1/12, and Jill's rate is 1/240.
  Let's assume that Jill takes t hours to finish the remaining work.

  Simplifying the equation, we get:
  1/4 + 1/240 * t = 1/3
  1/240 * t = 1/3 - 1/4
  1/240 * t = 1/12
  t = 12
  Therefore, it takes Jill 12 hours to finish the remaining work.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 70 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Mr.Sam takes 17 hours to go by train to a certain city and return by car. He loses 4 hours if he goes both ways by train. How long would he have taken if he had traveled by car in both ways?
Choices:
  A: 22 hrs
  B: 18 hrs
  C: 16 hrs
  D: 20 hrs
  E: 13 hrs
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the time taken by Mr. Sam to travel to the city by train is 'x' hours.
  Therefore, the time taken by Mr. Sam to return by car is also 'x' hours.
  According to the problem, Mr. Sam takes 17 hours to go by train to the city and return by car.
  Therefore, the total time taken by Mr. Sam = time taken to go by train + time taken to return by car
  Total time taken = x + x = 2x
  According to the problem, Mr. Sam loses 4 hours if he goes both ways by train.
  Therefore, the time taken by Mr. Sam to go both ways by train = 17 + 17 - 4 = 30 hours
  The time taken by Mr. Sam to go by car both ways = Total time taken - Time taken to go both ways by train
  Time taken by Mr. Sam to go by car both ways = 2x - 30
  We need to find the time taken by Mr. Sam to travel by car in both ways.
  Therefore, we need to find the value of 2x - 30.
  Let's solve for x.
  x + x = 17
  2x = 17
  x = 8.5
  Therefore, the time taken by Mr. Sam to go by car both ways = 2x - 30 = 2(8.5) - 30 = 17 - 30 = -13
  The answer cannot be negative. Therefore, the answer is "None of the above".
Action: Answer("None of the above")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 71 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: For bringing each copper coin from the bottom of a river, a coin-diver gets 20 cents, and for each brass coin she gets 25 cents. If after one dive, she got $3.40. What is the minimum number of copper coins that she brought?
Choices:
  A: 4
  B: 3
  C: 2
  D: 1
  E: 0
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume that the diver brought x copper coins and y brass coins.
  The amount of money she gets for each copper coin is 20 cents, and she brought x copper coins, so the total amount of money she gets for copper coins is 20x cents.
  The amount of money she gets for each brass coin is 25 cents, and she brought y brass coins, so the total amount of money she gets for brass coins is 25y cents.
  The total amount of money she got after one dive is $3.40, which is equal to 340 cents.
  Therefore, we can write the following equation: 20x + 25y = 340
  We need to find the minimum number of copper coins that she brought, which means we need to minimize the value of x.
  Let's try to solve for x in terms of y: 20x = 340 - 25y => x = (340 - 25y)/20
  Since x has to be a whole number, we need to find a value of y that makes (340 - 25y)/20 a whole number.
  The only value of y that satisfies this condition is y = 2.
  If y = 2, then x = (340 - 25*2)/20 = 3.
  Therefore, the minimum number of copper coins that she brought is 3.
Action: Answer("B")

  The total amount of money she got after one dive is $3.40, which is equal to 340 cents.
  Therefore, we can write the following equation: 20x + 25y = 340
  We need to find the minimum number of copper coins that she brought, which means we need to minimize the value of x.
  Let's try to solve for x in terms of y: 20x = 340 - 25y => x = (340 - 25y)/20
  Since x has to be a whole number, we need to find a value of y that makes (340 - 25y)/20 a whole number.
  The only value of y that satisfies this condition is y = 2.
  If y = 2, then x = (340 - 25*2)/20 = 3.
  Therefore, the minimum number of copper coins that she brought is 3.
Action: Answer("B")
Votes: B, B, B, B, B, B, B, B, B, B
Agent Answer: B

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 72 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The sum of the digits of a three digit number is 17, and the sum of the squares of its digits is 109. If we subtract 495 from the number, we shall get a number consisting of the same digits written in the reverse order. Find the number.
Choices:
  A: 368
  B: 377
  C: 288
  D: 997
  E: 112
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the three digit number be represented by abc.
  Then, a + b + c = 17 and a^2 + b^2 + c^2 = 109.
  Also, 100a + 10b + c - 495 = 100c + 10b + a.
  Simplifying the above equation, we get 99a - 99c = 495, which gives a - c = 5.
  We can use the first two equations to solve for b and c in terms of a.
  From a + b + c = 17, we get b + c = 17 - a.
  From a^2 + b^2 + c^2 = 109, we get b^2 + c^2 = 109 - a^2.
  We can substitute b + c = 17 - a into b^2 + c^2 = 109 - a^2 to get:
  (17 - a)^2 - 2bc = 109 - a^2
  Simplifying the above equation, we get bc = (a - 4)(a - 8)/2.
  Since a, b, and c are digits, we know that 0 <= a, b, c <= 9.
  We can use this fact to try different values of a until we find a solution that satisfies all the conditions.
  We can start with a = 9 and work our way down.
  If a = 9, then bc = 20, which is not possible since b and c are digits.
  If a = 8, then bc = 12, which gives b = 3 and c = 4.
  If a = 7, then bc = 5, which is not possible since b and c are digits.
  If a = 6, then bc = 2, which is not possible since b and c are digits.
  If a = 5, then bc = 0, which is not possible since b and c are digits.
  If a = 4, then bc = 4, which gives b = 2 and c = 2.
  Therefore, the three digit number is 422, and the answer is (422 + 495) = 917.
  The answer is D: 997.

Question: Fernando purchased a university meal plan that allows him to have a total of 3 lunches and 3 dinners per week. If the cafeteria is closed on weekends and Fernando always goes home for a dinner on Friday nights, how many options does he have to allocate his meals?
Choices:
  A: 5C3*4C3
  B: 5C4*4C2
  C: 5C2*4C4
  D: 5C6*4C5
  E: 4C3*4C3
Response 0:
Thought:
  Fernando has 3 lunches and 3 dinners to allocate.
  He goes home for dinner on Friday nights, so he only needs to allocate 2 dinners.
  He has 5 weekdays to allocate his 3 lunches and 2 dinners.
  He can choose 3 lunches out of 5 weekdays in 5C3 ways.
  He can choose 2 dinners out of 4 weekdays in 4C2 ways.
  Therefore, the total number of options is 5C3 * 4C2.
  The answer is A: 5C3*4C2.

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 74 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The ratio of the volumes of a cube to that of the sphere which will fit inside the cube is?
Choices:
  A: 2: π
  B: 7:2
  C: 8:2
  D: 6: π
  E: 8:3
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let the side of the cube be 'a'.
  The diameter of the sphere will be equal to the side of the cube.
  The volume of the cube is a^3.
  The volume of the sphere is (4/3)πr^3, where r = a/2.
  The ratio of the volumes of the cube to the sphere is a^3 : (4/3)π(a/2)^3.
  Simplifying this expression, we get 6 : π.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 6: π.
Action: Answer("D")

  The ratio of the volumes of the cube to the sphere is a^3 : (4/3)π(a/2)^3.
  Simplifying this expression, we get 6 : π.
  Therefore, the answer is D: 6: π.
Action: Answer("D")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 75 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: There are ten lime soda bottles on a table in a restaurant. They are to be served among two different groups of customers consisting of 5 members each. How many ways are there to create these 2 groups?
Choices:
  A: 90
  B: 105
  C: 126
  D: 252
  E: 525
Response 0:
Thought:
  We need to find the number of ways to divide 10 lime soda bottles into two groups of 5 each.
  The first group can be formed in 10C5 ways (10 choose 5).
  The second group can be formed in 5C5 ways (5 choose 5).
  Therefore, the total number of ways to create these 2 groups is (10C5) * (5C5) = 252.
  The answer is D: 252.
Action: Answer("D")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 76 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: All 250 files on Sam's hard drive are infected by either a virus or a worm or both. The number of files that are infected only by a worm is 2.5 times the number of files that are infected by both a virus and a worm. If 50% of the files were not infected by a virus, how many of Sam's files were NOT infected by a worm?
Choices:
  A: 50
  B: 70
  C: 75
  D: 100
  E: 125
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's use a Venn diagram to represent the information given in the problem.
  Let's use the following variables:
    - w: number of files infected only by a worm
    - v: number of files infected only by a virus
    - b: number of files infected by both a virus and a worm
  From the problem, we know that:
    - w = 2.5b
    - v + w + b = 250
    - v = 0.5(250) = 125 (since 50% of the files were not infected by a virus)
  We can use the first two equations to substitute for w and b in terms of v:
    - w = 2.5b = 2.5(250 - v - b)
    - b = (250 - v - w)/2.5 = (250 - v - 2.5b)/2.5
  Substituting these expressions for w and b into the equation v + w + b = 250, we get:
    - v + 2.5b + (250 - v - 2.5b)/2.5 = 250
    - 2.5v + 5b + 250 - 2v - 5b = 625
    - 0.5v = 125
    - v = 250/2 = 125
  Therefore, there are 125 files that are not infected by a virus.
  We can use the equation w = 2.5b to find that b = 50.
  We can use the equation v + w + b = 250 to find that w = 75.
  Therefore, there are 75 files that are not infected by a worm.
Action: Answer("C")

### Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 77 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A trader sold an article at a profit of 20% for Rs.360. What is the cost price of the article?
Choices:
  A: 270
  B: 300
  C: 280
  D: 320
  E: 315
Response 0:
Thought:
  Let's assume the cost price of the article is x.
  The trader sold the article at a profit of 20%, which means the selling price is 120% of the cost price.
  Selling price = 120% of cost price = (120/100)*x = 1.2x
  The selling price is given as Rs.360.
  Therefore, 1.2x = 360
  Solving for x, we get x = 300.
  Therefore, the cost price of the article is Rs.300.
Action: Answer("B")
